dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cerberus MS REST API</h1><a id="user-content-cerberus-ms-rest-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cerberus MS REST API" href="#cerberus-ms-rest-api"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A Django REST Framework API service for the Cerberus security platform, providing comprehensive threat modeling and data flow diagram (DFD) management capabilities with Neo4j graph database integration.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h2><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Cerberus MS REST API is the backend service that powers the Cerberus security platform. It provides a robust REST API for managing threat models, data flow diagrams, security components, and threat analysis. Built with Django REST Framework and Neo4j, it offers powerful graph-based threat modeling capabilities.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features</h2><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 <strong>Core Functionality</strong></h3><a id="user-content--core-functionality" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 Core Functionality" href="#-core-functionality"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Threat Modeling</strong>: Complete STRIDE threat analysis and management</li>
<li><strong>Data Flow Diagrams</strong>: Visual representation of system architecture</li>
<li><strong>Component Management</strong>: Process, DataStore, and ExternalEntity components</li>
<li><strong>Trust Boundaries</strong>: Security boundary definition and management</li>
<li><strong>User Management</strong>: Multi-user project collaboration</li>
<li><strong>Bulk Operations</strong>: Efficient bulk data synchronization</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔧 <strong>Technical Features</strong></h3><a id="user-content--technical-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔧 Technical Features" href="#-technical-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Django REST Framework</strong>: Robust API framework with automatic documentation</li>
<li><strong>Neo4j Integration</strong>: Graph database for complex relationship modeling</li>
<li><strong>OpenAPI Documentation</strong>: Auto-generated API documentation with Swagger UI</li>
<li><strong>CORS Support</strong>: Cross-origin resource sharing for web applications</li>
<li><strong>Docker Support</strong>: Containerized deployment with health checks</li>
<li><strong>Graph Visualization</strong>: Cypher queries for comprehensive diagram analysis</li>
</ul>

</ul>

<li><code>POST /api/diagrams/{diagram_key}/import/</code> - Import diagram data</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Health &amp; Documentation</h3><a id="user-content-health--documentation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Health &amp; Documentation" href="#health--documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>GET /api/health/</code> - Health check endpoint</li>
<li><code>GET /api/schema/</code> - OpenAPI schema</li>
<li><code>GET /api/docs/</code> - Swagger UI documentation</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prerequisites</h3><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prerequisites" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Python 3.11+</li>
<li>Docker and Docker Compose</li>
<li>Neo4j database (see <a href="/man-anr/cerberus-ms-rest/blob/cerberus-graph-db">cerberus-graph-db</a> for setup)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h3><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Clone the repository:</strong></li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/yourusername/cerberus-ms-rest.git
cd cerberus-ms-rest"><pre>git clone https://github.com/yourusername/cerberus-ms-rest.git
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> cerberus-ms-rest</pre></div>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Set up environment:</strong></li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Create virtual environment
python -m venv env
source env/bin/activate  # On Windows: env\Scripts\activate

# Install dependencies
pip install -r requirements.txt"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Create virtual environment</span>
python -m venv env
<span class="pl-c1">source</span> env/bin/activate  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> On Windows: env\Scripts\activate</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install dependencies</span>
pip install -r requirements.txt</pre></div>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Configure environment variables:</strong></li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Create .env file
cp .env.example .env
# Edit .env with your Neo4j connection details"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Create .env file</span>
cp .env.example .env
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Edit .env with your Neo4j connection details</span></pre></div>
<ol start="4" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Run database migrations:</strong></li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python manage.py migrate"><pre>python manage.py migrate</pre></div>
<ol start="5" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Start the development server:</strong></li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python manage.py runserver"><pre>python manage.py runserver</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Docker Deployment</h3><a id="user-content-docker-deployment" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Docker Deployment" href="#docker-deployment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Build and run with Docker Compose:</strong></li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker-compose up --build"><pre>docker-compose up --build</pre></div>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Access the API:</strong></li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>API: <a href="http://localhost:8000/api/" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:8000/api/</a></li>
<li>Documentation: <a href="http://localhost:8000/api/docs/" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:8000/api/docs/</a></li>
<li>Health Check: <a href="http://localhost:8000/api/health/" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:8000/api/health/</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration</h2><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration" href="#configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment Variables</h3><a id="user-content-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment Variables" href="#environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a <code>.env</code> file with the following variables:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-dotenv notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Neo4j Configuration
NEO4J_BOLT_URL=bolt://localhost:7687
NEO4J_USER=neo4j
NEO4J_PASSWORD=password1

# Django Configuration
SECRET_KEY=your-secret-key-here
DEBUG=True
ALLOWED_HOSTS=localhost,127.0.0.1

# CORS Configuration
CORS_ALLOWED_ORIGINS=http://localhost:3000,http://localhost:8080"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Neo4j Configuration</span>
<span class="pl-v">NEO4J_BOLT_URL</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">bolt://localhost:7687</span>
<span class="pl-v">NEO4J_USER</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">neo4j</span>
<span class="pl-v">NEO4J_PASSWORD</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">password1</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Django Configuration</span>
<span class="pl-v">SECRET_KEY</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">your-secret-key-here</span>
<span class="pl-v">DEBUG</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">True</span>
<span class="pl-v">ALLOWED_HOSTS</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">localhost,127.0.0.1</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> CORS Configuration</span>
<span class="pl-v">CORS_ALLOWED_ORIGINS</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">http://localhost:3000,http://localhost:8080</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Neo4j Connection</h3><a id="user-content-neo4j-connection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Neo4j Connection" href="#neo4j-connection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The API connects to Neo4j using the following configuration:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# In settings.py
NEOMODEL_NEO4J_BOLT_URL = os.getenv('NEO4J_BOLT_URL', 'bolt://localhost:7687')
NEOMODEL_NEO4J_USER = os.getenv('NEO4J_USER', 'neo4j')
NEOMODEL_NEO4J_PASSWORD = os.getenv('NEO4J_PASSWORD', 'password1')"><pre><span class="pl-c"># In settings.py</span>
<span class="pl-v">NEOMODEL_NEO4J_BOLT_URL</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">os</span>.<span class="pl-c1">getenv</span>(<span class="pl-s">'NEO4J_BOLT_URL'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'bolt://localhost:7687'</span>)
<span class="pl-v">NEOMODEL_NEO4J_USER</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">os</span>.<span class="pl-c1">getenv</span>(<span class="pl-s">'NEO4J_USER'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'neo4j'</span>)
<span class="pl-v">NEOMODEL_NEO4J_PASSWORD</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">os</span>.<span class="pl-c1">getenv</span>(<span class="pl-s">'NEO4J_PASSWORD'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'password1'</span>)</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project</h4><a id="user-content-project" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project" href="#project"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Diagram</h4><a id="user-content-diagram" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Diagram" href="#diagram"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

  <span class="pl-s">"rpo_hours"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1.0</span>              <span class="pl-c"># Recovery Point Objective</span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">API Usage Examples</h2><a id="user-content-api-usage-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: API Usage Examples" href="#api-usage-examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cypher Queries</h2><a id="user-content-cypher-queries" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cypher Queries" href="#cypher-queries"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The API integrates with Neo4j and provides powerful graph-based threat modeling capabilities. See <a href="/man-anr/cerberus-ms-rest/blob/main/cypher_queries.md">cypher_queries.md</a> for comprehensive query examples.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example: Get Complete Diagram</h3><a id="user-content-example-get-complete-diagram" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example: Get Complete Diagram" href="#example-get-complete-diagram"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cypher notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="MATCH (d:Diagram {key: &quot;dfd_v1&quot;})
OPTIONAL MATCH (d)-[:HAS_ELEMENT]-&gt;(n:DFDNode)
OPTIONAL MATCH (d)-[:HAS_THREAT]-&gt;(t:ThreatNode)
OPTIONAL MATCH (d)-[:HAS_TRUST_BOUNDARY]-&gt;(tb:TrustBoundaryNode)
RETURN d, collect(n) as components, collect(t) as threats, collect(tb) as trust_boundaries"><pre><span class="pl-k">MATCH</span> (<span class="pl-smi">d</span>:<span class="pl-smi">Diagram</span> <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-k">{</span><span class="pl-smi">key</span><span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s">"dfd_v1"</span><span class="pl-k">}</span></span>)
<span class="pl-smi">OPTIONAL</span> <span class="pl-k">MATCH</span> (<span class="pl-smi">d</span>)<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-k">[</span><span class="pl-en"><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-en">HAS_ELEMENT</span></span><span class="pl-k">]</span><span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span>(<span class="pl-smi">n</span>:<span class="pl-smi">DFDNode</span>)
<span class="pl-smi">OPTIONAL</span> <span class="pl-k">MATCH</span> (<span class="pl-smi">d</span>)<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-k">[</span><span class="pl-en"><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-en">HAS_THREAT</span></span><span class="pl-k">]</span><span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span>(<span class="pl-smi">t</span>:<span class="pl-smi">ThreatNode</span>)
<span class="pl-smi">OPTIONAL</span> <span class="pl-k">MATCH</span> (<span class="pl-smi">d</span>)<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-k">[</span><span class="pl-en"><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-en">HAS_TRUST_BOUNDARY</span></span><span class="pl-k">]</span><span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tb</span>:<span class="pl-smi">TrustBoundaryNode</span>)
<span class="pl-k">RETURN</span> <span class="pl-smi">d</span>, <span class="pl-c1">collect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">n</span>) <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">components</span>, <span class="pl-c1">collect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">t</span>) <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">threats</span>, <span class="pl-c1">collect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">tb</span>) <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">trust_boundaries</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example: Threat Analysis</h3><a id="user-content-example-threat-analysis" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example: Threat Analysis" href="#example-threat-analysis"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-cypher notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="MATCH (t:ThreatNode)-[:THREATENS]-&gt;(c:DFDNode)
WHERE t.criticality = &quot;high&quot;
RETURN t.name, t.threat_type, collect(c.name) as affected_components
ORDER BY t.criticality DESC"><pre><span class="pl-k">MATCH</span> (<span class="pl-smi">t</span>:<span class="pl-smi">ThreatNode</span>)<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-k">[</span><span class="pl-en"><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-en">THREATENS</span></span><span class="pl-k">]</span><span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span>(<span class="pl-smi">c</span>:<span class="pl-smi">DFDNode</span>)
<span class="pl-k">WHERE</span> <span class="pl-smi">t</span>.<span class="pl-smi">criticality</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"high"</span>
<span class="pl-k">RETURN</span> <span class="pl-smi">t</span>.<span class="pl-smi">name</span>, <span class="pl-smi">t</span>.<span class="pl-smi">threat_type</span>, <span class="pl-c1">collect</span>(<span class="pl-smi">c</span>.<span class="pl-smi">name</span>) <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-smi">affected_components</span>
<span class="pl-k">ORDER BY</span> <span class="pl-smi">t</span>.<span class="pl-smi">criticality</span> <span class="pl-k">DESC</span></pre></div>

</ol>

</ol>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Health Monitoring</h3><a id="user-content-health-monitoring" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Health Monitoring" href="#health-monitoring"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The API provides health check endpoints for monitoring:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>GET /api/health/</code> - Basic health check</li>
<li><code>GET /api/health/detailed/</code> - Detailed system status</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">With Cerberus Platform</h3><a id="user-content-with-cerberus-platform" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: With Cerberus Platform" href="#with-cerberus-platform"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This API integrates with other Cerberus components:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>cerberus-graph-db</strong>: Neo4j database backend</li>
<li><strong>cerberus</strong> (Flutter): Frontend application</li>
<li><strong>cerberus-gai-agents</strong>: AI-powered threat analysis</li>
<li><strong>cerberus-ms-guardrail</strong>: Security policy enforcement</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Python Client Example</h4><a id="user-content-python-client-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Python Client Example" href="#python-client-example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import requests

class CerberusAPI:
    def __init__(self, base_url=&quot;http://localhost:8000/api&quot;):
        self.base_url = base_url
    
    def create_project(self, key, name):
        response = requests.post(f&quot;{self.base_url}/projects/&quot;, json={
            &quot;key&quot;: key,
            &quot;name&quot;: name
        })
        return response.json()
    
    def get_diagram(self, diagram_key):
        response = requests.get(f&quot;{self.base_url}/diagrams/{diagram_key}/&quot;)
        return response.json()"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">CerberusAPI</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__init__</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">base_url</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"http://localhost:8000/api"</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">base_url</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">base_url</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">create_project</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">key</span>, <span class="pl-s1">name</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">post</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">base_url</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/projects/"</span>, <span class="pl-s1">json</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{
            <span class="pl-s">"key"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">key</span>,
            <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">name</span>
        })
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">json</span>()
    
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_diagram</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">diagram_key</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">base_url</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/diagrams/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">diagram_key</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/"</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">json</span>()</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">JavaScript Client Example</h4><a id="user-content-javascript-client-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: JavaScript Client Example" href="#javascript-client-example"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class CerberusAPI {
    constructor(baseUrl = 'http://localhost:8000/api') {
        this.baseUrl = baseUrl;
    }
    
    async createProject(key, name) {
        const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/projects/`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ key, name })
        });
        return response.json();
    }
    
    async getDiagram(diagramKey) {
        const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/diagrams/${diagramKey}/`);
        return response.json();
    }
